last updated 8/15/17

MFL.football

A responsive my fantasy league template from MFLaddons.

View demo

Template instructions

The template will make use of Home Page Messages. You may have already used these from previous years. Save any code you need from these on your computer and delete them from your MFL site before you get started. Also make sure that you don't have one of your HPM's set as a header or footer already as that will interfere with the installation.

If you have any questions with installation or have ideas, please post here.

If you are installing on a new site it may look something like this: If you already named your HPM's it may look a little different. In this example header would be #1, footer #2, homepage #3, message board #4, and so on...

  1. To install the template you'll need to log in as commish and go to the commish setup page.

  2. On the "Select a skin" page choose "none".

  3. CSS — Go to the "Images and Other URL's link and paste in one of the css files below.

    Couple dark version and a few light versions to choose from.

    DARK THEMES
black with yellow
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/dark/roboto-black-yellow.css

black with red
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/dark/roboto-black-red.css


LIGHT THEMES
blue and green
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-blue-green.css

blue and red
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-blue-red.css

blue and yellow
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-blue-yellow.css

black and red
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-black-red.css

black and green
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-black-green.css

black and light blue with a more light gray background
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-black-lightblue.css

darknavy and orange
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-darknavy-orange.css

blue-gray and orange - loosely based off SMF default message board theme
//mfl.football/assets/css/colors/light/roboto-smf.css

  4. Homepage — Copy all the code in the boxt below. This sets the layout of the homepage and includes a javascript file that allows you to log in. Paste into a HPM and label "homepage".

    Your HPM's may already be named so look for the 3rd link under "Home page message setup"
    <div class="row">
  <div class="col-md-4 col-md-push-8">
    <div class="utility-nav">
      <div class="utility-nav--button">
        <a href="//%HOST%/%YEAR%/options?L=%LEAGUEID%&O=133">
          <svg class="icon-exchange">
            <use xlink:href="#icon-exchange"></use>
          </svg>
          <div class="svg-text">Trade Block</div>
        </a>
      </div>
      <div class="utility-nav--button">
        <a href="//%HOST%/%YEAR%/home/%LEAGUEID%?MODULE=MESSAGE20">
          <svg class="icon-file-text">
            <use xlink:href="#icon-file-text"></use>
          </svg>
          <div class="svg-text">Rules</div>
        </a>
      </div>
      <div id="loginlink" class="utility-nav--button loginbutton">
        <svg class="icon-sign-in">
          <use xlink:href="#icon-sign-in"></use>
        </svg>
        <div class="svg-text"></div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <module name="TRADES" />
    <module name="LEAGUE_CHAT" COUNT="20" />
    <div class="hidden-xs hidden-sm">
      <module name="OWNER_ACTIVITY" />
      <module name="MY_NEWS" COUNT="10" />
      <module name="NEXT_WEEKS_FANTASY_SCHEDULE" />
    </div>
  </div>
  <div class="col-md-8 col-md-pull-4">
    <div class="mobile-standings-wrapper hidden-xs">
      <module name="STANDINGS" UNIT="DIVISION00" />
      <module name="STANDINGS" UNIT="DIVISION01" />
    </div>
    <div class="visible-xs visible-sm">
      <module name="BRIEF_STANDINGS" />
    </div>
    <module name="MESSAGE_BOARD_SUMMARY" COUNT="10" />
    <module name="POWER_RANK" DISPLAY="LEAGUE" />
    <div class="hidden-calendar">
      <module name="MONTHLY_CALENDAR" />
    </div>
    <div class="visible-xs visible-sm">
      <module name="MY_NEWS" COUNT="10" />
    </div>
    <module name="TOP_PERFORMERS" />
    <div class="visible-xs visible-sm">
      <module name="NEXT_WEEKS_FANTASY_SCHEDULE" />
      <module name="OWNER_ACTIVITY" />
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
<script src="//mfl.football/assets/js/homepage.js"></script>
    If you don't include this HPM you won't be able log in.

  5. Header — Copy all the code in the box below. This header includes jquery. Its also where you can edit your league name and the icons/navigation. Paste into a HPM and label "header".

    Don't forget to ✓ in header of all league pages

  7. Go to the homepage modules and tabs setup page. On the main tab add a new column at 100% and place the homepage HPM directly underneath.

  8. Remove all other modules from the main tab and delete all other tabs. This template will only use the main tab. Multiple tabs aren't supported.

    Once you are done you'll only have the main tab. All other tabs will be removed.
    Do not add any additional modules on this page. Adding modules will now be done by adding a snippet of code into the homepage message we added in step 4. You can find the code to add modules here.

  9. Take a look at your homepage. Then look at a few other pages. If everything look good...

Congratulations you installed the template!

Answers to the most common questions, and information about common customizations can be found below.

Still need some help?

MFL has a great community forum, someone is usally available to help answer any questions you may have.

Customize the header

How do I change my league name?

Look for this code and update it to change your league name. Look for the names "Your" "League" and "here". You can delete any of the spans if you don't need them <span class="leaguename--dotus">.com</span> 

<div class="leaguename">
    <span class="leaguename--the">Your</span><span class="leaguename--league">Name</span><span class="leaguename--dotus">here</span>
</div>

Then replace it with an image of your choice. Place the url for your league logo in the code below. Your new html will look something like this:

<div class="league_logo" id="league_logo">
 <img class="img-responsive" src="LINK TO MY NEW LEAGUE LOGO IMAGE">
</div>

Hint: Using the class img-responsive allows the image to scale on mobile devices automatically

<!-----  ADD  CAPTION AND WRAP TABS AND CONTENT IN TABLE TO MATCH SITE  ------>
<table id="custom-reports" class="report hidden-xs hidden-sm"><caption><span>Top Free Agents</span></caption>
 <tbody><tr><td>

<!-----  TABBED REPORT NAVIGATION  ------>
   <ul class="tabbed-reports">
    <li class="report31 current">MVP</li>
    <li class="report32">QB's</li>

    <li class="report36">PK's</li>
    <li class="report37">DEF</li>
   </ul>

   <div class="reports-content">
    <div class="report31"><center><module name="TOP_FA" COUNT="10"/></center> </div>
    <div class="report32" style="display:none;"><center><module name="TOP_FA" COUNT="10" POSITION="QB" /> </center></div>
    <div class="report33" style="display:none;"><center><module name="TOP_FA" COUNT="10" POSITION="RB" /></center> </div>

Live Scoring

The navigation has a link to HPM 13. You can follow the instructions on this page and add in the live scoring module to hpm 13.

Custom HPM template

If you have a custom message that you want to have the same style as the rest of the site you can follow this template and insert your info in the middle.

Example 
<table align="center" cellspacing="1" class="homepagemodule report" id="customhpm1">
  <caption><span>Custom HPM</span></caption>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>
        <!--insert your custom code here-->
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

Twitter

Display a twitter feed on your page. You can display a list or a specific profile. The data-link-color="#color" where #color is the color of your links. In this case #2e8743 is the green from the default color scheme.

Example 
<table align="center" cellspacing="1" class="homepagemodule report" id="twitter">
  <caption><span>Fantasy News</span></caption>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>
        <!--To customize replace the href="url" with another list or a specific account. href="https://twitter.com/MFLaddons/lists/fantasy-football"-->
        <a class="twitter-timeline" data-theme="light" data-link-color="#2e8743" href="https://twitter.com/MFLaddons/lists/fantasy-football"></a> <script async src="//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js" charset="utf-8"></script>
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

Tricks

For faster mobile-friendly development, use these utility classes for showing and hiding content by device via media query.

Try to use these on a limited basis and avoid creating entirely different versions of the same site. Instead, use them to complement each device's presentation.

A great use case is with the standings. There are 2 standings modules available, brief and standard. The brief one is perfect for mobile while the standard one works great on desktop and tablet.

Example 
<div class="mobile-standings-wrapper hidden-xs">
  <module name="STANDINGS" UNIT="DIVISION00" />
  <module name="STANDINGS" UNIT="DIVISION01" />
</div>
<div class="visible-xs-block">
  <module name="BRIEF_STANDINGS" />
</div>

In this example the brief standings is used on phones, while the standard standings broke out by division is used on desktops and tablets.

Available classes

Use a single or combination of the available classes for toggling content across viewport breakpoints.

Extra small devices Phones (<768px) Small devices Tablets (768px) Medium devices Desktops (992px) Large devices Desktops (1200px)
.visible-xs-* Visible Hidden Hidden Hidden
.visible-sm-* Hidden Visible Hidden Hidden
.visible-md-* Hidden Hidden Visible Hidden
.visible-lg-* Hidden Hidden Hidden Visible
.hidden-xs Hidden Visible Visible Visible
.hidden-sm Visible Hidden Visible Visible
.hidden-md Visible Visible Hidden Visible
.hidden-lg Visible Visible Visible Hidden

The .visible-*-* classes for each breakpoint come in three variations, one for each CSS display property value listed below.

Group of classes CSS display
.visible-*-block display: block;
.visible-*-inline display: inline;
.visible-*-inline-block display: inline-block;

So, for extra small (xs) screens for example, the available .visible-*-* classes are: .visible-xs-block, .visible-xs-inline, and .visible-xs-inline-block.




Contribute

The template is free to use. If you would like to help out with hosting/bandwidth or for future capabilities and color schemes please consider donating. Thanks!

Send a donation

You can also help but letting me know if you see bugs or would like to help contribute code to this project.

Updates

Accessiblity

I'm doing my best to keep the template and each color variation as accessible as possible so color schemes should work well if even if you are color blind. There's a good chance at least one person in your league is.

Built with

This template is built with Sass, uses Bootstrap's grid as well as a few extras from that framework. The goal is to make our My Fantasy League (MFL) site's work great on any device.
